data_BMOD-STAR.dic

#  version date -  2019-02-04


# Many of the following item type definitions and descriptions for units
# have been taken from the pdbx and mmCIF dictionaries.

# The BMOD-STAR dictionary has been constructed to be congruent with the pdbx
# where the data being modeled are equivalent. In these cases, where possible
# identical items have been used and the definitions for these items are
# intended to be identical.


# Some definitions: Tag is a combination of a category and an item
#                   Item describes the specific data item in the category
#                   Category is the grouping of items
#                   Category group is the grouping of item categories that 
#                      are encapsulated in a save frame
#                   Super category group is the grouping of save frame categories 
#                      by scientific area and entry information


save_datablock_description
    _Datablock.ID                BMOD-STAR
    _Datablock.Description
;
    This data block contains the BMOD-STAR dictionary.
;

save_


######################################################################

save_dictionary_header
    _Dictionary.Sf_category                dictionary_header
    _Dictionary.ID                         BMOD-STAR
    _Dictionary.description
;
     This data block contains the BMOD-STAR dictionary.
;

    _Dictionary.Title           BMOD-STAR.dic
    _Dictionary.Version         1.0.0.0

     loop_
       _Dictionary_history.Version
       _Dictionary_history.Update
       _Dictionary_history.Revision
       _Dictionary_history.Dictionary_ID
                    
     1.0.0.0          2019-02-04
;
     Original formal dictionary release.
;
BMOD-STAR

     stop_

 

######################################################################

     loop_
       _Super_save_frame_group.ID
       _Super_save_frame_group.Name
       _Super_save_frame_group.Description
       _Super_save_frame_group.Dictionary_ID

    1     entry_information
;
The entry_information category super group captures general information describing the entry, any study that the entry is a member, and information regarding the processing of the entry and updates to the entry after its initial release to the public.
;
BMOD-STAR

    2     citations
;
Citations referenced in the entry and the primary citation related to this specific entry.
;
BMOD-STAR

    3     molecular_assembly
;
The molecular_assembly super_group contains the complete chemical description of the molecular assembly studied, additional reference information for the molecular assembly and its components, and links to information for the equivalent or similar molecular assemblies or biopolymer components in other databases.
;
BMOD-STAR

    4     experimental_details
;
The experimental_details category super group captures information about the samples, sample conditions, NMR spectrometers, NMR experiments and other data regarding the experiments used to collect the NMR spectral data and to derive kinetic, thermodynamic, and structure information.
;
BMOD-STAR

    5     NMR_parameters
;
The NMR_parameters super group contains the category groups used to model NMR spectral parameters or theoretically calculated parameters like chemical shifts and links to supporting information.
;
BMOD-STAR

    6     structure
;
The structure category super group captures atomic coordinates, constraints, statistical data, and other related information.
;
BMOD-STAR

     stop_

######################################################################

     loop_
       _Save_frame_category.Name
       _Save_frame_category.Description
       _Save_frame_category.Super_save_frame_group_ID
       _Save_frame_category.Super_save_frame_group_name
       _Save_frame_category.Dictionary_ID

'entry_information'
;
General information about the entry; e.g. title, authors,, history,, etc.
;

     1     'entry_information'     BMOD-STAR

'citations'

Categories that provide bibliographic information for the citation for the entry.

     2     'citations'     BMOD-STAR

'chem_comp'

Categories that describe chemical components of entities and molecular assemblies.

Categories that describe a molecular assembly.
;

     3     'molecular_assembly'     BMOD-STAR

'sample'

;

     4     'experimental_details'     BMOD-STAR

Categories that describe the experimental conditions used in conducting individual scientific experiments.

     4     'experimental_details'     BMOD-STAR

Categories that describe computer software.

Categories that describe an NMR spectrometer.
;

     4     'experimental_details'     BMOD-STAR

'experiment_list'
;
Categories that describe a list of experiments.
;

     4     'experimental_details'     BMOD-STAR

'computing_platform'
;
Categories that describe a computer or computing facility or platform that involves high performance or high throughput computing.
;

     4     'experimental_details'     BMOD-STAR

'molecular_modeling_file_set'
;
Categories that describe a set of files generated to model the structure and other characteristics of a small molecule.
;

     6     'structure'     BMOD-STAR

'chem_shift_reference'
;
Categories that capture information about the compounds and parameters used to reference NMR chemical shifts.
;

     5     'NMR_parameters'     BMOD-STAR

'assigned_chemical_shifts'
;
Categories that capture assigned chemical shift values and links to the samples, sample conditions, NMR experiments, and other information about how the assigned chemical shifts were derived.
;

     5     'NMR_parameters'     BMOD-STAR

'spectral_peak_list'
;
Categories that capture the properties of NMR spectral peaks, spectral parameters, and links to the NMR experiments and other information regarding the data.
;

     5     'NMR_parameters'     BMOD-STAR

     stop_

####################
## ITEM_TYPE_LIST ##
####################
#
#
#  The regular expressions defined here are not compliant
#  with the POSIX 1003.2 standard as they include the 
#  '\n' and '\t' special characters. These regular expressions
#  have been tested using the version 0.12 of Richard Stallman's
#  GNU regular expression libary in POSIX mode. 
#
#                                                                            
# For some data items, a standard syntax is assumed. The syntax is           
#   described for each data item in the dictionary, but is summarized here:  
#                                                                            
#   Names:     The family name(s) followed by a comma, precedes the first    
#              name(s) or initial(s).                                        
#                                                                            
#   Telephone numbers:                                                       
#              The international code is given in brackets and any extension 
#              number is preceded by 'ext'.                                  
#                                                                            
#   Dates:     In the form yyyy-mm-dd.                                       
#                                                                            
##############################################################################


     loop_
       _Item_type.Code
       _Item_type.Primitive_code
       _Item_type.Construct
       _Item_type.Detail
       _Item_type.Dictionary_ID

               code      char
               '[_,.;:"&<>()/\{}'`~!@#$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-]*'
;
              code item types/single words ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               ucode      uchar
               '[_,.;:"&<>()/\{}'`~!@#$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-]*'
;
              code item types/single words  (case insensitive) ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               line      char
               '[][ \t_(),.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%?+=*A-Za-z0-9|^-]*'
;
              char item types / multi-word items ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               uline      uchar
               '[][ \t_(),.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%?+=*A-Za-z0-9|^-]*'
;
              char item types / multi-word items (case insensitive)...
;
BMOD-STAR
               text      char
               '[][ \n\t()_,.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%?+=*A-Za-z0-9|^-]*'
;
              text item types / multi-line text ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               int       numb
               '-?[0-9]+'
;
              int item types are the subset of numbers that are the negative 
               or positive integers.
;
BMOD-STAR
               float     numb
               '-?(([0-9]+)[.]?|([0-9]*[.][0-9]+))([(][0-9]+[)])?([eE][+-]?[0-9]+)?'
;
              int item types are the subset of numbers that are the floating
               numbers.
;
BMOD-STAR
               name      uchar
               '_[_A-Za-z0-9]+\.[][_A-Za-z0-9%-]+'
;
              name item types take the form...
;
BMOD-STAR
               idname    uchar
               '[_A-Za-z0-9]+'
;
              idname item types take the form...
;
BMOD-STAR
               any       char
               '.*'
;
              A catch all for items that may take any form...
;
BMOD-STAR
               yyyy-mm-dd  char
                '[0-9]?[0-9]?[0-9][0-9]-[0-9]?[0-9]-[0-9][0-9]'
;
               Standard format for CIF dates.
;
BMOD-STAR
               uchar3    uchar
              '[+]?[A-Za-z0-9]?[A-Za-z0-9][A-Za-z0-9]'
;
               data item for 3 character codes
;
BMOD-STAR
               uchar1    uchar
              '[+]?[A-Za-z0-9]'
;
               data item for 1 character codes
;
BMOD-STAR
               yes_no   char
               '(yes)|(no)'
;
               data item for boolean codes that have values of 'yes' or 'no'
;
BMOD-STAR
               symop    char
               '([1-9]|[1-9][0-9]|1[0-8][0-9]|19[0-2])(_[1-9][1-9][1-9])?'
;
              symop item types take the form n_klm, where n refers to the
               symmetry operation that is applied to the coordinates in the
               ATOM_SITE category identified by _atom_site_label.  It must
               match a number given in _symmetry_equiv_pos_site_id.

               k, l, and m refer to the translations that are subsequently
               applied to the symmetry transformed coordinates to generate
               the atom used.  These translations (x,y,z) are related to
               (k,l,m) by
                     k = 5 + x
                     l = 5 + y
                     m = 5 + z
               By adding 5 to the translations, the use of negative numbers
               is avoided.
;
BMOD-STAR
               atcode      char
               '[][ _(),.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%?+=*A-Za-z0-9|^-]*'
;
              Character data type for atom names  ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               yyyy-mm-dd:hh:mm  char
    '[0-9]?[0-9]?[0-9][0-9]-[0-9]?[0-9](-[0-9]?[0-9])?(:[0-9]?[0-9]:[0-9][0-9])?'
;
               Standard format for CIF dates with optional time stamp.
;
BMOD-STAR
               fax      uchar
               '[_,.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-]*'
;
              code item types/single words  (case insensitive) ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               phone      uchar
               '[_,.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-]*'
;
              code item types/single words  (case insensitive) ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               email      uchar
               '[_,.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-]*'
;
              code item types/single words  (case insensitive) ...
;
BMOD-STAR
               int-range       numb
               '-?[0-9]+(--?[0-9]+)?'
;
              int item types are the subset of numbers that are the negative 
               or positive integers with optional range.
;
BMOD-STAR
               float-range     numb

'-?(([0-9]+)[.]?|([0-9]*[.][0-9]+))([(][0-9]+[)])?([eE][+-]?[0-9]+)?(--?(([0-9]+)[.]?|([0-9]*[.][0-9]+))([(][0-9]+[)])?([eE][+-]?[0-9]+)?)?'
;
              int item types are the subset of numbers that are the floating
               numbers.
;
BMOD-STAR
       
#
               binary    char
;
\n--CIF-BINARY-FORMAT-SECTION--\n\
[][ \n\t()_,.;:"&<>/\{}'`~!@#$%?+=*A-Za-z0-9|^-]*\
\n--CIF-BINARY-FORMAT-SECTION----
;
;
              binary items are presented as MIME-like ascii-encoded
               sections in an imgCIF.  In a CBF, raw octet streams
               are used to convey the same information.
;
BMOD-STAR

# BMOD-STAR additions

              framecode   char
              '[.;:"&<>(){}'`~!$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-][_.;:"&<>(){}'`~!$%A-Za-z0-9*|+-]*' 
;
             A value that points to a save frame.
;
BMOD-STAR

    stop_
